formable_nations_mod_category = {
	no_cosmetic_tag = {
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
		cost = 0
		visible = { 
			is_ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_options_formable_nations }
			has_country_flag = unform_available
		}
		days_re_enable = 0
		
		icon = generic_decision
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = unform_available }
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = formable_nations_old_capital
				}
				clr_state_flag = formable_nations_old_capital
				ROOT = { set_capital = { state = PREV } }
			}
		}
	}
	####################################################################
	formable_nations_africa = {#continent
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				 
			}
		}
		
		cost = 0  days_re_enable = 0
		
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = unform_available }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = hide_formable_nations }
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = no_limit
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { 
				tooltip = africa_requirement_tooltip 
				OR = {
					AND = {
						all_state = {
							OR = {
								AND = {
									is_on_continent = africa
									NOT = {
										OR = {
											state = 697
											state = 178
											state = 702
											state = 703
											state = 704
											state = 297
											state = 705
											state = 708
											state = 709
											state = 706
											state = 707
											state = 713
											state = 543
											state = 906
										}
									}
									is_controlled_by = ROOT
								}
								NOT = { is_on_continent = africa }
								state = 697
								state = 178
								state = 702
								state = 703
								state = 704
								state = 297
								state = 705
								state = 708
								state = 709
								state = 706
								state = 707
								state = 713
								state = 543
								state = 906
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_ai = no
						has_global_flag = debug_mode
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { tooltip = not_already_existing_tt NOT = { any_country = { has_cosmetic_tag = FORM_AFR } } }
		}
		icon = formable_nations_africa
		complete_effect = { capital_scope = { set_state_flag = formable_nations_old_capital }
			set_cosmetic_tag = FORM_AFR
			custom_effect_tooltip = core_land
			hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus  set_country_flag = unform_available
				every_state = {
					limit = { 
						is_on_continent = africa
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

		icon = formable_nations_greater_japan

		allowed = {
			original_tag = JAP
		}

		available = {
			is_subject = no
			
			###GAUNGXI STATES
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = southern_china_requirement_tt ####QUANGXI
				controls_state = 593
				controls_state = 592
				controls_state = 599
				controls_state = 594
				controls_state = 591
			}
			JAP_is_intigrating_china = yes
		}
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 120
		visible = {
			original_tag = JAP
			NOT = { has_global_flag = integrated_southern_china }
			has_country_flag = JAP_can_now_integrate_china
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_intigrating_china
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = JAP_intigrating_china
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_imperial_ambitions_met }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_imperial_ambitions_met
					add_idea = JAP_imperial_ambitions_met_1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_imperial_ambitions_met_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_imperial_ambitions_met_1
					add_idea = JAP_imperial_ambitions_met_2
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_production }
					modify_timed_idea = {
						idea = JAP_production
						days = 30
			  }
			}
			else = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = JAP_production
					days = 30
				}
			}
			##GUANGXI
				593 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				592 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				599 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				594 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				591 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = integrated_southern_china
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	formable_nations_khmer_empire = {
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				  
			}
		}
		
		cost = 0  days_re_enable = 0
		
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = unform_available }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = hide_formable_nations }
			OR = { 
				has_global_flag = no_limit
				original_tag = CAM
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = modern_country }
		}
		
		available = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					
					count_triggers = {
						amount = 5
						741 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
						289 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
						868 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
						869 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
						670 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					has_global_flag = debug_mode
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { tooltip = not_already_existing_tt NOT = { any_country = { has_cosmetic_tag = FORM_KHM } } }
		}
		icon = formable_nations_khmer_empire
		complete_effect = { capital_scope = { set_state_flag = formable_nations_old_capital }
			set_cosmetic_tag = FORM_KHM
			custom_effect_tooltip = core_land
			hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus  set_country_flag = unform_available
				741 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				289 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				868 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				869 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
				670 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			724 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
			286 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
		}
	}

	formable_nations_americas = {#continent
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				  
			}
		}
		
		cost = 0  days_re_enable = 0
		
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = unform_available }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = hide_formable_nations }
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = no_limit
				capital_scope = { OR = { is_on_continent = north_america  is_on_continent = south_america } }
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					
					all_state = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								OR = { is_on_continent = north_america  is_on_continent = south_america }
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										state = 696
										state = 101
										state = 739
										state = 299
										state = 720
										state = 649
										state = 690
										state = 689
										state = 686
										state = 694
										state = 308
										state = 692
										state = 315
										state = 318
										state = 319
										state = 730
									}
								}
								is_controlled_by = ROOT
							}
							NOT = { OR = { is_on_continent = north_america  is_on_continent = south_america } }
							state = 696
							state = 101
							state = 739
							state = 299
							state = 720
							state = 649
							state = 690
							state = 689
							state = 686
							state = 694
							state = 308
							state = 692
							state = 315
							state = 318
							state = 319
							state = 730
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					has_global_flag = debug_mode
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { tooltip = not_already_existing_tt NOT = { any_country = { has_cosmetic_tag = FORM_AME } } }
		}
		icon = formable_nations_americas
		complete_effect = { capital_scope = { set_state_flag = formable_nations_old_capital }
			set_cosmetic_tag = FORM_AME
			set_capital = { state = 304 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = core_land
			hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus  set_country_flag = unform_available
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = { is_on_continent = north_america is_on_continent = south_america }
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	formable_nations_germany = {
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				  
			}
		}
		
		cost = 0  days_re_enable = 0
		
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = hide_formable_nations }
			OR = { 
				has_global_flag = no_limit
				original_tag = PRE
				original_tag = HAN
				original_tag = MEK
				original_tag = SAX
				original_tag = SHL
				original_tag = AUS
				original_tag = BAY
				original_tag = WUR
			}
			OR = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = FORM_NGF
				has_cosmetic_tag = FORM_SGF
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			has_war = no
			OR = {
				AND = {
					
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = formable_nations_germany_tt
						count_triggers = {
							amount = 19
							5 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							42 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							50 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							51 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							52 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							53 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							54 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							55 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							56 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							57 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							58 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							59 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							60 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							61 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							62 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							63 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							64 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							65 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							66 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							67 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
							68 = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					has_global_flag = debug_mode
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { tooltip = not_already_existing_tt NOT = { any_country = { has_cosmetic_tag = GER } } NOT = { country_exists = GER } }
		}
		icon = formable_nations_germany
		complete_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER
			set_capital = { state = 64 }
			hidden_effect = { sound_effect = complete_focus
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
					GER = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = fascism
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 10
							neutrality = 10
							fascism = 70
							communism = 10
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = communism
					}
					GER = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = communism
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 10
							neutrality = 10
							fascism = 10
							communism = 70
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
					GER = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = democratic
							elections_allowed = yes
						}
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 70
							neutrality = 10
							fascism = 10
							communism = 10
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					GER = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = neutrality
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 10
							neutrality = 70
							fascism = 10
							communism = 10
						}
					}
				}
				GER = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
				GER = {
					annex_country = {
						target = ROOT
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
